 THE THREE ADMIRALS. CHAPTER ONE. THE DRAGON OFF THE BONINS--A CONVERSATION BETWEEN TOM ROGERS AND ARCHIE GORDON--GERALD DESMOND ON THE SICK-LIST--THREATENINGS OF A TYPHOON--IT STRIKES THE SHIP--SHE RUNS BEFORE IT--THE SHIP HOVE TO--THE BOWSPRIT CARRIED AWAY--A MARINE WILL-OF-THE-WISP--ENTER A BAY IN ONE OF THE BONIN ISLANDS--TOM, GERALD, AND BILLY GET LEAVE TO VISIT THE SHORE--A BEAUTIFUL CAVERN--LAND ON THE ISLAND--THEIR DISCOVERIES--FISHING-- INTERRUPTED BY SHARKS--A PICNIC--BOAT DRIFTS AWAY FROM THE SHORE--TOM SWIMS OFF--NARROW ESCAPE FROM A SHARK--SEE THE SHIP IN THE OFFING--PULL AFTER HER--A HURRICANE COMING ON--FEARFUL DANGER WHEN RE-ENTERING THE HARBOUR. Her Majesty's corvette _Dragon_, lately commanded old friend Jack Rogers, superseded Commander Rawson, her passage across wide Pacific, bound Esquimault harbour, Vancouver's Island, Japan, she sent despatches. The wind fair, screw rest, she sail, looking trim taunt little man-of-war sailor's heart could desire. Her stay Japan short, leave granted, even officers seen little country people; though, hoped return long, much matter. As great importance _Dragon_ soon get back Vancouver's Island, Commander Rawson received directions visit Ladrone Islands, somewhat southward his course, order obtain particulars outrage, said committed English subject mongrel inhabitants islands, centuries belonged Spain. The smooth sea shone brightly rays sun, undimmed cloud mist. In directions snowy wings sea fowl could seen, dipping towards ocean, rising blue ether, showing land great distance. As wind northward, air cool, though shady side ship generally sought watch deck, except whose heads seemed impervious hot rays tropical sun. Two midshipmen slowly pacing port side quarter-deck, feet shade afforded shelter heat. The one, somewhat short, well-knit lad, open countenance, well tanned, blue laughing eyes, his whole appearance giving promise strength activity; other, tall youth sandy hair, pleasant features well freckled. Though tall, he well built called lanky, showed he possessed strength activity. "I say, Archie, I envy fellows _Eolus_ going China; see sorts fun, Celestials sure give hurry. The _Eoluses_ sort work brother Jack cousin Murray went last Chinese war, midshipmen." The speaker Tom Rogers, youngest brother Captain Jack Rogers; his companion Archie Gordon, Captain Alick Murray's cousin. "Gerald dreadfully cut able remain board _Eolus_, instead come back us return home; Captain Adair's letter peremptory, and, newspapers say, I hope he hear something his advantage. Gerald would better pleased his uncle let know he sent for." "He great complain, seeing climate China none delectable, he would run risk shot bargain," observed Archie. "I wish I chance going home, finding possessor tidy fortune title." "But there is honour glory, fun, pig-tails captured, loot, chance serving naval brigade seeing work shore, _Shannon's_ people India, fair prospect promotion end it." "If body happens shot, ye ken," observed Archie, who, though every bit eager Tom sort work he described, took pleasure differing opinion whenever he could. "We not, however, bother poor Desmond subject he well again," said Tom. "I really believe he fell sick vexation, though he happy enough us more." "He much better to-day," remarked Archie, "and I hope to-morrow doctor let come deck again, although he may fit duty day two more." Mr Mildmay, first lieutenant, officer watch, paced deck, spyglass hand, going bridge sweeping horizon his glass, he frequently called look-outs forecastle fore-yardarm keep eyes open. Jos Green, master, also continually there, else consulting chart his cabin, part ocean comparatively little known, cruel reefs might exist, marked down. "The first lieutenant master seem fidgety," remarked Tom. "So would be, I suspect, responsibility navigating ship rested us," answered Archie. "After all, one suffers sufficiently careful; that is rule cousin gave I first came sea." "And good rule is, too, doubt that," observed Tom. "My brother Jack careful his ship, everything connected her, old lady her best silk gown Sunday morning, though one, hear talk, would suppose he harum-scarum fellow alive, always excepting his old shipmate, Captain Adair. He is, however, staid steady enough reality. I glad hear he got his post rank time brother Jack did; three old messmates, delight call themselves, post-captains, day, I hope, admirals. I wish, however, wait long. Your grave cousin Murray fit admiral he twenty years hence, and, unless fine fellows die off, take best part time get flag." "It encouragement us, though," observed Archie; "for posted without great amount interest, may hope get promoted consequence good conduct." "Yes, remember seen great deal service, piping times peace return, may find hard matter get employed able exhibit good conduct." "Weel, mon, we will hope best, may nation kindly think fit come fisticuffs old England, give us something do," said Archie. "There is every chance that, I think," said Tom. Just seven bells struck afternoon watch. "I will go see Gerald getting on, I come deck again; it is dull work lying himself." Tom found his old messmate, whose cot slung little way outside berth, he might advantage air coming after-hatchway, sucking lustily orange he grasped one hand, he held book other. He absorbed perusal he notice Tom. Suddenly he burst loud fit laughter. "Capital fun; I liked seen it!" he exclaimed; "soused head ears second time. Ah, ah, ah!" "What is joke?" asked Tom. "I have got old Peregrine Wiffle tumbles water second time, he showing he saw small fish playing wharf, picked boat-hook." Tom Gerald good laugh together. "You do not seem bad," observed Tom. "No; fever, whatever was, got hold me, cut stick, though I do not feel quite nimble I ought be," answered Gerald. "I believe disappointment going China, thinking uncle Terence want home for, climate, hot sun, anything else, I intend ask doctor let go deck to-morrow, time I shall finished book, I want look islands may happen pass. There curious shaped ones, I told." "Yes; sighted some. One seemed rise three four hundred feet pointed peak, right water, not, I say, eighth mile circumference. It marked chart Lot's wife. A solitary existence she must lead herself." "Whereabouts we?" asked Desmond. "At noon, passing curious rock, latitude 29 degrees north, longitude 14 degrees east. We shall next sight Bonin Islands, Rosario, another lofty island, little rock, standing sea." "Do ask doctor I may get up, Tom; I sorry pass places without look them," exclaimed Desmond. "I finish book by-and-by." Just officer spoken of, Mr Hussey, came gun-room. He short, somewhat stout gentleman, good-natured expression countenance, merry twinkle eye, showed he could enjoy joke, likely utter many one himself. His naturally florid complexion deepened still ruddy hue exposure hot suns tropics. "Do, doctor, let get up; physic done immense deal good, I feel quite well already," said Desmond. The doctor felt his pulse. "You get up!" he exclaimed. "What think made of?" trying look grave. "Arrah, shure, sugar spice that is nice! that is midshipmen made of. But shure, doctor dear, keep here, stewing myself, I might enjoying pure air heaven?--for I really well, doctor." "You mean say finished book, got tired lying bed," reply. "Well, promise good boy keep shade, may dress go deck, I cannot undertake scratch sick-list yet." "Thank you, sir," said Desmond; "I everything tell me, take much medicine think fit prescribe. I want duty yet, I have got hundred pages `Tom Cringle's Log' read, I cannot gallop book people do." "Well, well, possibly ship may manage take care without you," said doctor, he passed on. Whereupon Desmond began put his clothes, task he accomplished Tom's assistance. He felt himself, however, much weaker he expected, he made his way upon deck, though he tried hard show he again. He received friendly greeting his messmates, Mr Mildmay congratulated able make his appearance. There plenty amuse taste natural history even land sight, doctor, great naturalist, constantly _qui vive_, sea teemed squid, medusae, polypi, flying-fish. Several latter came ports, general scramble them, midshipmen, watch active, coming largest share. A short time afterwards unhappy fish made appearance, well fried, mess-table. Whales, too, sporting directions, tempted locality abundance food before-named creatures afforded. Several old whalers among crew could scarcely restrain impatience, and, could obtained leave, would gone gear could prepared attack monsters deep. Since _Dragon_ left Japan, weather remarkably fine, calms light winds. But calms lasted scarcely long enough fires lighted ship sail. That evening, however, long heavy swell began come north-east; undulations rapidly increasing size, making ship roll side side, her chains touched water. Desmond, common two three his messmates, ship's boys marines, began feel uncomfortable. "What is going happen?" he asked; "I am mighty quare region stomach." "I suppose going gale wind, change," answered Tom, never ill since he first came sea. "We shall shorten sail, I have notion, long, prepared blustering Boreas, he thinks fit visit us." The whole appearance sky sea quickly changed. The wildfowl, hovering around ship, winged flight nearest islands shelter could found. The atmosphere pervaded peculiar glare rays sun coming clouds dull ochreous red, giving ocean, ship, her canvas sides, unnatural tint. As summits swells, till smooth glass, rose higher higher, formed crests foam, sparkled ruddy light, like masses jewels. Hitherto sufficient wind steady ship she made her way amid heaving billows. Mr Jay, second lieutenant, officer watch; he made sign Tom. "Rogers," he said, "go tell commander weather getting much worse." "Be quick it, too," exclaimed Green; "there time lose." Commander Rawson quickly deck. After taking rapid glance round, he shouted out, "All hands shorten sail." The watch came tumbling deck. The topsails lowered, topmen, like bees, swiftly swarmed aloft, laying yardarms. "Hold teeth eyelids, Billy," said Tom his old friend Billy Blueblazes, he sprang his station main-top. The canvas speedily reduced closely-reefed fore main-topsails fore-staysail. It hard work hold on, ship rolled even violently before. The wind, however, come soon expected, impossible say moment might strike her. That would come ordinary strength, without warning, every reason believe. The crew, performed task, called deck. There something appearance sea sky, heaviness atmosphere, made even toughest old seaman feel extraordinary depression spirits, though he might suspected because. "Faith! I am sorry I remain quietly cot," said Desmond; "it seems world coming end. I surprised see flames spouting sea. It looks big fires burning away it." "Do not ken, Gerald, water would putting fire out," observed Archie; "though appearance islands fire enough one time other. They raised ocean volcanic agency." "I disposed dispute truth remark," said Desmond; "I wish sea would get quiet, let us glide comfortably it, instead kicking disturbance." While midshipmen speaking, ship continued her uneasy course, slowly rising summit huge billow gliding deep trough. Suddenly loud roar heard, seemed mighty monster deep struck prodigious blow side ship. Over she heeled water rushed her lee ports. "Up helm. Furl main-topsail. Take another reef fore-topsail. We must run it," cried commander, hoping steer clear islands reefs might ahead. The ship quickly rose even keel, dashed forward amid foaming seas, rolling, however, even violently before. So rapidly waves follow, many struck her stern; not, however, her dead lights closed. So tremendous blows, seemed her masts would shaken her. The doctor purser, sitting gun room, thrown seats sprawling table, fully believing ship struck rock, hands would soon struggling lives. As soon things could got rights, Tom helped Desmond below, he glad enough turn his hammock, he anxious quit. "Shure got Harry Cane aboard us, Mr Rogers," observed Tim Nolan, Tom's watch, took liberty old shipmate address his officer freedom others would ventured. They stationed together forecastle, looking ahead. "I wish gentleman would good enough take off, then," answered Tom, "or he may playing us scurvy trick, sending craft ugly reefs abound hereabouts." "We will keeping bright look-out that, sir," said Tim. "We may reef see it," observed Tom. "For part, I believe Providence steering us, I comfortable." The ship continued drive gale. The second lieutenant came forward, he confess his eyes little value pierce dark gloom ahead. The foam-crested waves could alone seen, rapidly rising falling. Tom's eyes ached. He sorry he relieved. Still, neither he one else felt inclined go below; one could tell might happen. The thick clouds hung like dark canopy, apparently masts' heads. The thunder, rumbling distance, began roar loudly, flashes forked lightning came zig-zagging air, threatening every instant strike ship. But, though played round sides, none touched her. The commander ordered fires got up, ship might steam, ready emergency. Hour hour typhoon continued howl even fiercely first. Frequently blast would strike ship, making her tremble solid mass hurled her. Then would come lull seconds, another blast would suddenly strike her way made every plank shake throughout her frame. Even hardy board wished day. The morning light brought abatement gale. Onward went ship, plunging vast hollow, threatened engulf her; she rose rapidly top another sea, either side appeared vying other, could leap highest accomplish her destruction. The officers gathered aft, men waist, holding firmly stanchions, anything could secure themselves. Each time ship plunged her head seas, masts bent, every moment would go board. At length lull came, commander, consulted Green, fearing dangers ahead, determined bring ship to, operation attended considerable risk, sea striking her moment might sweep her deck. A favourable opportunity waited for. The crew stood ready lower fore-topsail hoist main-topsail, closely reefed. Both tasks accomplished; officers anxiously watching seas ship rode them, happily she safely rounded to, lay her main-topsail mast, though scarcely she got position, fierce foam-crested sea, roaring up, struck her bows deluged her decks, shaking herself clear, like thing life, she sprang forward, water rushed ports. The lull continued, many hoped gale breaking; less hour another furious squall struck ship, nearly laid her her beam ends. Once she rose, her stout canvas stood severe trial put, she rode comparative ease minutes. The seas, however, seemed become broken ever. A prodigious one came roaring towards weather bow. The _Dragon_ appeared see her danger, struggled avoid it, next instant she pitched headlong deep hollow, another monstrous wave, rising apparently half high foretop, fell completely her deck. For seconds, her commander his officers feared she would never rise. No orders could issued, nothing could done. The crew stood silently stations, uttering word, showing felt fearful predicament placed. The ship remained, were, fixed sea; sudden jerk she burst her way it, her stout bowsprit broken short off, next sea threw wreck across forecastle. The commander's voice heard tones vying howling gale. The crew, obedient his orders, rushed forward secure bowsprit lashings; boatswain, another gang, lost moment setting fresh stays, prevent foremast carried away. This, loss one boats, forepart bulwarks stove in, chief damages hitherto received _Dragon_ gale. It over, however. Again sun set, wind continued rage unabated fury. The watch ordered turn in, officers done so, and, though tired out, still remained deck. Tom Archie standing aft, close together, latter suddenly grasped Tom arm. "Oh, mon! what is that?" he exclaimed, pointing main-topmast head, appeared crowned ball pale fire. "It curious appearance; though I never saw before, brother Jack told it. It sort Jack-of-lantern, Will-of-the-wisp, or, Gerald called it, `Saint Vitus' dance.' I believe he meant say Saint Elmo's fire." While midshipmen gazing up, flame descended rapidly mast, running first along main topgallant yardarm, returning, came, main-topsail yard, glided extreme end. Here rested seconds, made mind next do. Presently back came mast, darted lee yardarm. It yet finished journey. Once gliding back, ascended mast, made way main-topmast stay, foremast went gliding backwards forwards along yard. "I wish would come deck, might chance catching it," said Tom. "I read somewhere man going aloft bucket, clapped light, brought prisoner. It sort gas driven air finds something rest on. Why goes moving curious way I do not know, anybody else, I believe. I wish doctor deck,--he would tell us." "Shall I call him?" asked Archie. "I do not think he would thank you," said Tom. "Let rest quiet; perhaps he get his clothes fire disappeared." Tom right. In another minute luminous ball, gathering point, shot upwards vanished. "That is good sign," heard Green observe first lieutenant; "we shall gale breaking long." Before watch hurricane sensibly decreased, showing master right his prognostication. The sea continued, however, tumble ship terribly morning dawned, clouds began disperse, sun rose appeared fly his burning rays. By noon sky perfectly clear, when, observation taken, commander determined run lee one Bonin Islands, sighted shortly afterwards. Steam got up, vessel made rapid way, though she continued roll considerably, moved glass-like swell, still came north-east, showing that, although calm rested waters she was, storm raged another part ocean. Several islands seen rising water port bow, _Dragon_ drew near trees could distinguished hills, showing barren appeared distance. Rounding southern end one them, she went half speed, feeling her way lead she opened sheltered bay two high projecting points. Running she brought within quarter mile shore perfectly still water. Everybody glad enough rest tumbling last days. They allowed, however, enjoy many minutes' quiet; hands speedily set work repair damages. "We thankful escaped easily," observed Archie Gordon, surveying shore his telescope. "Look there, Tom, tall trees stretched ground roots air; must taken pretty hard blow break down. I see stumps sticking up, showing others snapped wind. It mercy weathered well did." Tom took glass. "I sorry them," he answered, "and I hope poor fellows living shore, would run great risk crushed. It makes think old song-- "`A strong nor'-wester's blowing, Bill; Hark I do not ye hear roar now? Lord help  them, I pities Unhappy folks shore now!' "I hope commander let us take run shore, however, sail." In course couple days repairs nearly finished, good deal painting done, commander resolved remain anchor another day. Green second lieutenant employed time surveying island, surveys complete. "I say, Gerald, must get trip way other," said Tom Desmond. "You would better run ashore, I am sure, suggested idea doctor, he say so, get Mr Mildmay let us boat." Gerald followed Tom's advice. "Of course, boy," answered good-natured doctor; "if find anything curious, remember bring me." "That I will, sir," said Tom. The doctor spoken first lieutenant, Tom went boldly asked use jolly-boat. "You her; remember must board good time," answered Mr Mildmay. Tom his party quickly ready, carrying fishing-lines, well baskets bring wild fruit might happen find. Tom Gerald making preparations, Billy Blueblazes came gun-room. "Holloa!" he exclaimed; "I have got leave go you. I suppose you will take grub?" "We will afther finding shore," answered Desmond; "game, fish, fruit. I propose carry couple muskets; shall sure find something other." "Elephants rhinoceroses," suggested Billy. "Not quite big beasts are," answered Tom. "We find rather cumbrous stow away game-bags." "But we will take bread, rum, cold beef--they likely grow island, events; potatoes either, pot boil in," remarked Desmond. The articles fancied would required quickly collected. "Shure, have not forgotten powder shot!" exclaimed Desmond, committing things charge Tim Nolan, accompany them, he might stow away boat. Pat Casey, Irishman saved savages, Jerry Bird, formed crew boat. Bird Nolan tried, steady men. Casey, accustomed savage life, might useful searching fruits animals might found island. He also first-rate fisherman, plenty experience his residence Indians. The party shoved soon second lieutenant master left ship. "The thing I am sorry Archie us," said Tom. "However, sure plenty fun sort other." At end bay small piece sandy beach, towards Tom steered boat. As surf, ran her it, stepped without difficulty. A nearer acquaintance, however, showed country tempting character first supposed. There trees close beach, broken two storm, lay prostrate ground. Even larger trees, species mahogany, lay uprooted directions, found difficult make way among them. Still, dint climbing fallen trunks, cutting road brushwood, made progress, discovered circle rocky hills, many places almost precipitous. It seemed almost hopeless attempt climbing them, especially Desmond acknowledged he "did feel well sort work," would likewise carry muskets, provisions cooking utensils. "As much time lose, I propose go back boat, try find another landing-place along coast," said Tom. His plan agreed to; launching boat, took oars. After rounding rocky point, formed eastern side bay, pulled along distance hopes finding another landing-place, whence could make way interior. As surf, sea perfectly smooth, kept close land. In many places high cliffs rose precipitously water. As pulled along foot one cliffs, Tom shouted out-- "Holloa! there is big cavern directly ahead us; water seems run right it, I surprised could get distance boat." They stopped rowing, survey mouth cavern. It appeared upwards thirty feet height almost width. Everybody, course, eager explore cavern; rowing gently, risk might run knocking bows boat rock, made way cavern. By keeping oars moving, boat glided on. Ahead, darkness, impossible ascertain far cave penetrated land. As soon eyes got accustomed subdued light existed distance thirty forty feet entrance, beauties grotto began dawn sight. Glittering stalactites, thousand fantastic forms, hung high vaulted roof, either side appeared columns arches like ancient temple, tinted numberless delicate hues, extreme points stalactites glittering like bright gems reached reflected rays sun, penetrated far depths beneath, illuminating every object glassy surface. So beautifully clear water, party boat looked sides, could see right bottom cavern, appeared consist masses rock, forming caves hollows, covered richest marine vegetation. Here corals various tints, blue yellow, red white: amid ocean fan expanded vast leaves; lowest depths sprang sea-green stems fucus, twining round columns sank far down, afforded support. Here feathery tufts green vegetables floated upwards clear water, others various strange shapes hues formed recesses arches, twisted knotted variety ways. Fish, varied forms brilliant colours, darted among openings, rising close boat, curious ascertain character visitors submarine palace. "I wish doctor tell us names," exclaimed Tom. "Look there, odd creatures. What be?" The fish he pointed flat, oval form, rich silvery colour, delicately striped downwards azure bands. They swam perpendicular position, aided two long slender fins, one curving upwards back, considerable length, curving downwards opposite side. There many others differing form, beautiful colours, darting gliding out, but, apparently less curious timid disposition excited Tom's astonishment, venture near boat. There cray-fish, too, large size, enormous crabs, star-fish, sea-urchins, bivalves various sorts clinging rocks, open mouths, catch unwary creatures coming within reach. After enjoying scene time, giving strokes oars midshipmen allowed boat proceed cavern. Most party hanging water noses surface, hands trying catch fish might venture near, cry Tim made spring up. "Shure, he will afther catching us, do not look out," exclaimed Irishman, moment saw rising far depths cavern enormous shark, his eyes glaring like two glowing coals, open jaws he came nearer nearer boat. "He will swallowing whole us," cried Tim. "Back water! back water!" To Irishman shark probably appeared much larger really was. "He will not us harm; keep oars water," said Tom, was, course, obeyed, shark glided alongside boat, he kept eyeing suspicious glances. "Would afther wishing one us?" asked Desmond. "Then I hope you will mistaken; unless, Billy, wish kind baste, let arm treat." "Thank you," said Billy; "I would rather not. It would not give much trouble bite off, though." "We must disappointed expectation exploring cavern brute like that," exclaimed Tom. "Hand boat-hook." Standing up, he struck point his might nose monster, instant sank suddenness made Tom lose his balance, Desmond Billy seized he would overboard. "He is afraid us him," said Tom. "Now let us get far cavern can." They pulled cautiously on, Tim standing bows, feeling ahead boat-hook. The mouth cavern seemed grow smaller smaller, point light remained. Suddenly Pat Casey, pulling Jerry Bird, declared he felt something seize blade his oar. "It is shark, perhaps," said Tom. "We muskets ready. I will give shot, make keep his distance. Wait he tries again." Tom took musket, stood ready fire. "There! he is got oar his jaws," cried Pat. Tom fired. The flash revealed instant sides roof cavern, seemed glitter studded thousands jewels, ahead pitchy darkness, showing yet got extremity. The sound report, greatly increased loudness, went echoing amid arches pillars, died away far distance, proving great extent cavern. Whether shark hit not, impossible say; bullet tore point Pat's oar, showing Tom taken good aim. Jerry Bird suggested midshipmen would prudent pull back, without torches could see going. There might be, could tell contrary, big sea monster squatting end, might crunch without ceremony. Though Tom apprehensions score, he agreed return, proposing, _Dragon_ remain anchor another day, explore cave supply torches. The boat accordingly cautiously pulled round, made her way towards mouth. It curious watch arch growing higher higher, light gradually increasing. They almost reached entrance, when, either side, one, several sharks, came gliding up. One, bolder bigger rest, seized blade oar, crunching end; men keep watchful eye save destroyed. Tom fired musket, declared bullet went shark's head. As monster appear worse it, Desmond Billy doubted fact. Not Tom fired several times, boat got considerable distance cavern, sharks leave her. "There is one thing certain: that is place bathe in, would pleasant tumble overboard hereabouts," observed Tom, gravely. "I never see black monsters, wicked eyes, floating near looking one, without feeling uncomfortable." They row farther expected. At last saw narrow opening reef rocks, within made small bay, sandy shore, could land ease draw boat. The country beyond, too, looked far tempting yet seen. The water passage deep, difficulty making way bay. As yet seen nothing second lieutenant's master's boats, which, supposing island small size, expected meet coming round opposite side. "We shall probably see cut directly across island," observed Tom. They disappointed bay. The beach exactly wished for. They hauled boat up, agreed she could left without danger. "But I hope fellows going begin long march without food," observed Billy, noted his excellent appetite. "We game, caught fish. It is lucky brought food, I advised." Wood collected, fire quickly made. As brought cold meat bread them, potatoes cook. This operation superintended Tim, rest party searched productions island might add repast. They gone far Tom exclaimed-- "Why, cocoa-nut trees, fine ones, too. I thought none island." "They cocoa-nut trees, sure enough," said Desmond, "and cocoa-nuts growing them. How get question, stems stout allow us swarm up." "`Where there is there is way'; must climb, way other," said Tom, never liked beaten. On reaching spot, found cocoa-nut trees, yams bananas, covering ground wildest profusion, latter climbing surrounding branches, ripe fruit hung temptingly down. On examining further, discovered remains fence, showing ground enclosed, purpose forming garden, probably distant period. The yams, growing wild, likely worth much, bananas, notwithstanding latitude, appeared fine. In vain, however, gazed cocoa-nuts. Jerry, though active man, vowed he could attempt reach top unless could get rope one branches. While discussing matter, Pat Casey, helping Tim, came up, also caught sight cocoa-nut trees distance. "Bedad, I will afther it," he exclaimed; running back boat, he returned three four fathoms rope. This he twisted huge grummet round tree, leaving space enough his body get also. What dismay find, reaching it, boat, hauled up, floated rapidly rising tide, strong gust wind driven her considerable distance shore, she drifting off. Not moment lost. Tom felt he guilty act indiscretion remaining long shore, seen boat properly secured. He forgotten huge monsters sharks, prowling about, one way boat could regained. Somebody must swim her. These thoughts rapidly passed his mind. The swim nothing; he often swum ten times without fatigue. But sharks! He recollected shudder passed he seen approach boat two hours before. Without saying anything, he quickly thrown his clothes. "Shout, you, loud can," he exclaimed. "Good-bye, Desmond; good-bye, Billy," he said, shaking hands. "If I swallowed one brutes, say happened I duty." Without another word, Tom plunged in, rest party, rushing forward knees, began splashing water about, shouting top voices. "I cannot let go alone," said Jerry Bird, soon he saw midshipman about. Throwing his jacket shirt, he followed Tom, shouting lustily. "I coming, Mr Rogers," he cried; "you climb one side boat, I other." Tom within couple fathoms boat, his horror he saw dark fin, rising water. It stationary, however. Perhaps savage brute merely surveying boat, wondering strange creature was. Tom, undaunted sight, swam on. He might manage scramble board shark caught sight him. "Do lose heart, Bird," he cried out, he guessed his companion would seen shark's fin; "the chances he will not attack two us." A strokes more, Tom got hold gunwale boat; Jerry seized side. Tom, way fatigued, easily held up, and, got his left leg over, drag other, Jerry threw tilted boat side he on. It fortunate movement, shark ran his snout side, missing Tom's foot almost hair's breadth. Tom felt brute's head strike boat, well knew happened. It made draw his breath quickly; he work him. Without stopping moment, he Jerry, seizing oars, rapidly pulled boat back beach. Their companions gave way hearty cheer reached it. "Thank Heaven, escaped," said Desmond. "I saw happened; heart sank low I thought would never get right place. However, `a miss good mile'; sooner away better." Tom's Jerry's clothes handed boat, dressed themselves, rest party pulled bay. "I vote eat fish it is warm," said Billy Blueblazes, whose appetite (as Gerald used say him) "no dangers could daunt." "Just hand slice, I will eat I pull." This proposal seconded looks men, Tom accordingly passed portions, biscuit, forward. The crew ate fish gusto. They wise doing, might long pull them. Another another gun heard. "Those guns fired harbour," observed Tom; "the ship must put sea." Gerald agreed him; yet reef, ran across mouth bay, concealed her sight. The wind lately blowing quarters--now harbour, directly across it--until length heavy squall came entrance. "We shall strong wind teeth, pretty heavy pull," observed Tom Gerald. "I wish spent much time here; I shall justly get blame, anything happens." "It will not much matter gets blame happen drowned," answered Gerald. "However, known gone direction, captain probably stand along shore pick us up; chances shall safe board within hour so." The men bend backs oars force boat heavy seas came rolling narrow entrance. Under circumstances, Tom would put back waited improvement weather; signal recall peremptory, he considered his duty try get board risks. The sea, calm pulled along coast, tossed heavy foam-crested billows, came rolling rapid succession, bursting loud roars rock-bound shore, casting sheets spray reef. "We must heave cargo overboard," said Tom, he saw heavy seas come tumbling in. "The lighter boat better." The fish, hoped regale shipmates, quickly thrown overboard. "Shure, fine feast giving sharks," observed Desmond, he engaged work. They retained, however, dozen cocoa-nuts, case might required food. So slow progress made sea wind, almost dusk got clear land. Tom keeping look-out westward, side he expected ship appear. "There she is," he exclaimed length; "but she sail, standing south-east, I see smoke coming her funnel." Gerald agreed Tom case. They asked Jerry Bird, oldest seaman board, give his opinion. "You are right, sir," he said; "to mind something happened machinery. Either shaft piston rod broken, cannot get screw work. The commander, course, like remain bay, chance hurricane blowing right it; he got steam, probably standing along shore look us, accident, whatever was, happened; chance he saving ship go stand course he doing. Maybe he come long look us." Tom Gerald sure commander would desert them, time felt far comfortable seeing ship great distance off. The wind rapidly increasing; seas came rolling far heavily before, spray foaming crests sent boat, soon thoroughly wetted hands. This, course, one cared much about; question whether small boat would live furious sea likely encounter got board. If Jerry Bird right, ship herself must endeavour get good offing island case hurricane come on. Of seemed every probability. The gloom night rapidly increased, could distinguish ship light she showed her quarter. Was intended signal them, two boats yet returned her? As night advanced, weather became worse worse. "It is old rascal Harry Cane his tricks again," cried Tim; "I wish he waited bit, let us get comfortably board." "Never complain, Tim," observed Pat; "maybe shall glad have not left boat; got harbour lee, plenty grub shore, that is many poor fellow wished for, able find." Tom Gerald excessively anxious get board, determined persevere long possibly could. The men strained oars hearty good will. Now boat mounted one sea, rapidly descend trough another. Tom steered her carefully, keeping her head seas. He full well knew moment one heavy tops seas falling board might swamp her. Bird frequently looked his shoulder anxious glance. "Beg pardon, Mr Rogers, will not do," he said length; "the keener put run back harbour, better chance shall living night; happened ship I cannot tell. But, it is blowing like this, dead shore, shall not get board to-night to-morrow either." Tom Gerald length saw Jerry Bird right. They could longer distinguish _Dragon's_ lights. Either thick mist arisen, she got far seen; indeed, shore itself, boat sank hollow sea, invisible. "We must look smooth, pull boat round, lads," cried Tom. "Arrah! shure, hard matter find," said Tim Nolan, himself. Watching opportunity, Tom, trough sea, got boat round. "Give way, lads! give way!" he shouted out. Not necessity saying that; men knew well enough lives depended pulling hard could. Any moment sea, rolling astern, might break them. Tom stood look entrance harbour, he believed must approaching, he could see nothing one unbroken line foam bursting reef. The land rose shores bay. On highest part Tom recollected observed large clump tamana trees, which, pulled harbour, he noted good land-mark entering. In daylight could easily seen, darkness he could scarcely hope make sky, boat tumbled rolled way she doing. Still, hope; she strike reef either side entrance, she must instant dashed pieces, hands washed amidst foaming breakers. "Now, Desmond, use eyes never before, try see clump trees, find passage." Gerald strained his eyes. "I think I see dark spot almost ahead," he said length. "If do, must entrance," observed Tom. "I see other; chance; boat live long sea getting up." Tom steered towards point Gerald indicated. On sped boat. The loud roar breakers neared shore almost deafened them, Gerald, though sitting next Tom, shout make hear. "That is passage, I am sure it," he cried out. "You are right," answered Tom. "Give way, lads!" The boat rushed on. A tremendous sea, huge crest foam, came roaring astern, threatened overwhelm her. The men saw it, redoubled efforts. On either side rose wall white foam dashing directly rocks beneath fishing. An instant later boat would swamped; she flew, surrounded spray, another minute floating comparatively smooth water within sheltering reef. At moment hurricane burst forth, sending breakers flying sheets reef, howling fearfully went rushing amid trees forest, tearing huge limbs, laying many low, vivid flashes lightning followed peals rattling thunder, adding yet wild uproar elements. "Thank Heaven, safe!" exclaimed Gerald. "We may rightly acknowledge that; become boats old barkey?" said Tom. CHAPTER TWO. LAND--BURY THE BOAT--TAKE SHELTER UNDER A ROCK--THE HURRICANE RAGES--THE NIGHT PASSES BY--DESMOND SHOOTS AT A WILD BEAST--STORM ABATES--NO SHIP-- BOAT MISSING--BOAT DISCOVERED--TIM'S PORK CHOPS--DIGGING OUT THE BOAT-- PAT CHARGED BY A WILD BOAR--FLAG-STAFF SET UP--NO SHIP APPEARS--A HUT BUILT--EXPLORE THE ISLAND--MISS THE HOGS, BUT KILL SOME BIRDS-- PREPARATIONS FOR THE VOYAGE--TURTLE--BILLY'S EXPLOIT--LEAKY CONDITION OF THE BOAT--SEARCH FOR PITCH--TOM AND DESMOND SET OUT TO EXPLORE THE ISLAND. Tom steered boat bay towards beach lately left. It longer afforded easy landing place, waves came rolling in, even narrow entrance, creating surf sandy shore, scarcely her stern touched beach sea burst board, wetting every one through, nearly washing several articles her. All hands therefore jumped out. "Now, lads, long pull, strong pull, pull together," cried Tim. In another minute boat hauled beach, began taking things carrying spot left fire burning. Fortunately, muskets ammunition, though wet, saved, articles value boat, together compass Tom thoughtfully brought, although hitherto use it. The ashes fire still alight, found exposed beach spot would exactly wish encamp. "We must find sheltered place, put tent," said Tom Desmond. "A high overhanging rock would suit us best, will not tall mahogany trees, may moment crash upon heads, already specimen likely behave." "I would rather get snug cavern, discover one," said Desmond. "But found dark?" "I will soon twist couple torches I used make I Prime Minister Cannibal Islands," cried Pat Casey. "I think could find way left, I saw big rocks morning, I surprised find tolerable shelter them." "We ought soon possible," observed Tom, "for shall probably rain upon us many minutes over,--and hurricane begun, must remember. Get torches made soon can. Before leave must look boat, haul her farther beach; impossible say high water may rise hurricane setting shore." They accordingly hurried back ran boat feet farther up, beyond found impossible move her. "If leave her she is, she will sure blown away," observed Jerry Bird. "If I may advise, sir, I would make sort dock round her, fill her sand, sink her it. It cost us little trouble clear again, better her knocked pieces." Tom Desmond highly approved Jerry's proposal. All hands, therefore, set work boat stretchers make dock, easily quickly accomplished. They filled her sand, almost gunwale. "She steady enough now, sir," said Jerry. As soon work finished, returned former encampment, carrying boat's mast, yards, sails, oars them, assist forming tent, rest her gear placed safety high bank. Pat quickly twisted torches fibre cocoa-nuts, loading property, set out, he leading way. Scarcely commenced march, felt almost taken feet; loud crash heard, fell large tree, close were, torn roots. Happily weather side. They hurried on, keeping much possible open ground. Another blast came redoubled fury, almost blowing Pat's torches, burnt, indeed, much rapidity, seemed little probability able reach point towards steering, light. They gone far two torches burnt out. Heavily laden were, could move fast. Tim Nolan alone staggering boat's sail, oar, musket, basket provisions. Jerry Bird breaker water hung his back, equally heavily laden. It great relief Tom he heard Pat shout out, "Here rocks, though sign cave I see." "Perhaps, skirt along them, may find still sheltered place this," observed Tom. The party accordingly moved on, Pat announced his torch beginning burn his fingers, found recess rocks, well sheltered wind, although would obtain protection rain begin fall. The end torch afforded sufficient light collect sticks fire, light able put tent. The side rock affording back, made slope rock ground, heaviest rain would run off. There room hands get it, closely packed; fatigues day, thankful obtain shelter. As far, indeed, concerned, reason complain. They shelter, fire, food, water. "Let us see brought, Billy?" said Gerald. Billy produced three fish, he hung his back. "I thought want something supper, always wise carry one's grub one," he observed. "Much obliged forethought," said Gerald; Tim Pat summoned cook fish. The fire made close rock, much influenced wind. In short time Tim announced supper ready, "smoking hot," bottle rum produced provision basket. "Now, lads," said Tom, he poured liquor. "I want stint grog, recollect small supply, belief may many days get back ship, glass apiece I give you." The grog mixed, seamen, young officers, sat round fire, thinking little past future. The fish pronounced excellent; sipped grog one alternately spun yarn sang song. Tom Rogers must excepted. He felt his responsibility commanding party, he could get consciousness he ought returned earlier hour ship. This thought weighed his spirits, although he tried allow his companions discover his uneasiness. He felt also anxious ship. If Jerry Bird right supposing accident happened machinery, she might, hurricane, exposed greatest possible danger; she wrecked, might remain many months island, could find opportunity escaping. Tom, he came sea, often read living desert island one two pleasant companions, thought would good fun. When reality rose vividly him, he could confess he would rather keeping watch board, prospect returning home see his father, mother, friends. When, however, came his turn sing, he trolled forth, his rich deep voice, "Cease, rude Boreas," sea song character, he anxious thoughts trouble him. The blazing fire kept served dry clothes. When, hour later, rain came down, will not tropics, crept tent, taking care carry muskets things would damaged wet them. Tom, spite his fatigue, lay awake time. He thankful safe shore, able find sheltered position encampment. The wind roared howled terrific manner among forest trees. The earth seemed shake, would topple high rock them; although branches, sometimes large shrubs, torn roots, flew heads, none fell tent. Sometimes, several minutes together, crash succeeded crash, huge trees levelled ground. Then would come lull, wind would whistle mournfully, rather moan, recommence roaring lustily ever. Tom wondered his companions could sleep soundly amid uproar. The light fire, came side tent, fell forms stretched heads rock; while, lulls tempest, he could hear snoring away concert. He sufficiently well acquainted natural history Pacific Islands aware wild beasts interfere them, excepting hogs, whose traces seen; he every reason believe island uninhabited. He thought possible, however, rocks top cliff, loosened hurricane, might come tumbling heads; earth small branches hitherto fallen, he hoped would continue places. At events, even he his companions move away, likely find secure shelter. Should refuge sought trees, might prove still treacherous. He kept eye fire, fearing sudden blast might whisk embers tent; but, canvas thoroughly wet, would take time burn. He got two three times, and, standing his back cliff, he avoided rain poured torrents scarcely foot front him. Excepting glare fire cast upon white tent one side, black rocks other, shrubs front, pitchy darkness, though, looking upwards, he could distinguish tops trees waving fro sky. "I pray dear old _Dragon_ may escaped this!" he ejaculated once, hurricane, apparently renewed strength, hurled island. At length Desmond roused up. "You must two hours' watch more. Tom," he said. "Just lie get snooze; may long pull us, will not much room sleeping boat." Tom, sorry relieved, lay down, Desmond took his place. How long Tom sleeping he could tell, he rest party aroused shot fired close oars, and, looking up, saw Desmond musket his shoulder, he discharged. "What fire at?" asked Tom. "At bear, wolf, big baste other, shure," answered Desmond. "Whatever shall find out, cannot far off. I hit it, I certain that, gave terrible growl, bolted back bushes." The fire time almost burnt out, giving forth faint glow, scarcely afforded light sufficient see objects except close them, would useless attempt searching wild beast Desmond asserted he shot. He acknowledged he dropped asleep, that, suddenly awakening, he seen animal's eyes glaring ten yards off. Tom, looking his watch declining light fire, saw nearly dawn. A change better occurred. The strength hurricane much abated, though tree tops still waved backwards forwards wind whistled howled amid branches, abated breath, rain completely ceased. On looking up, small spaces clouds could seen, which, there, star glittered brightly. Jerry Bird, ought watch before, took Desmond's place, party settled wait morning. Sailors accustomed short snatches sleep. Even half hour less rest despised, less minute eyes closed happy forgetfulness were. Tom required calling; he scarcely forgotten his sleep happened, sooner pale light early morn driven away darkness night, than, opening his eyes, he crept tent Bird, dropped off. "I let rest sleep on, see things look," he said himself. As he made his way fallen trunks towards bay, he kept looking discover accessible part hill, he might climb summit rock, whose shelter slept, he supposed highest point thereabouts, order he might obtain wide view ocean around. He length found part, whence little climbing he might reach top hill. He began his ascent, he heard Desmond's voice shouting him, sitting he waited his messmate come up. The rock rugged uneven first supposed. Sometimes Desmond helped ledge, he hauled Desmond him. Here shrubs grew crevices rock, assisted ascent. At last stood together top. On casting eyes around, could nowhere see ship; indeed, scarcely expected she would sight. As far eye could range southward eastward, foam-crested giant waves leaped down, already motion becoming less rapid, seemed tumbling lazily slowly other, weary late exertions, though breakers incessantly burst rocky coast, sending masses foam flying far inland. "Even ship appear, likely able get her to-day," observed Desmond, pointing entrance bay, seas came tossing foaming. "It seems wonder got last night." "We may indeed thankful heaven swamped," said Tom; "but I surprised find, within hours, ship appear, get her. There scarcely time sea go since hurricane ceased blowing; I hope boats got board, run great risk lost." "Perhaps shipmates landed," observed Desmond; "and shall meet long. I glad know certain Archie Jos Green Mr Joy safe, though terrible thing think ship may cast away." "We hope best," answered Tom; "and go see boat fared. I somewhat anxious her, though I do not see could secured her better did." The descent nearly difficult climb hill, ran great risk, leaping rock rock, slipping tumbling dozen feet time next level. They nearly reached bottom, saw Billy Blueblazes Jerry Bird looking towards them. The countenances wore aspect dismay. "What happened?" asked Tom. "The boat gone!" answered Billy; "we cannot see her anywhere, even bit her wreck." "Faith! that is bad news," exclaimed Desmond; "but look everywhere? for, remember, everywhere means good wide space." "No, go right spot, use that," answered Billy. "Then will, perhaps may discover signs may indicate direction she driven," said Tom. They accordingly set off. Tom observed Billy failed do, shape beach greatly altered, wind driven sand far higher usual, parts risen height bank grass shrubs grew. Indeed, portion grassy ground covered sand. "What shall without boat?" cried Billy; "we shall spend lives here, I suppose, ship lost, men say think she little chance escaping." "I hope wrong conjectures," answered Tom; "and boat, I quite certain she lost, although may trouble finding her." On arriving part beach boat left, Tom looked round every direction, examined carefully bushes herbage along edge beach. "If she driven direction, she would broken bushes, appear injured," he observed. "Now, let us see whereabouts she lay. Do think tell, Bird?" The seaman examined ground. "I remember coming clump bushes these, directly I left her; look there, sir, her rudder stretcher," he enumerated articles belonging boat. Then stepping back, he said, "I am sure hereabouts she lay." "Then, depend upon it, shall find her. Do not see sand blown her, she safe enough within it. To save trouble, dig line parallel beach, another right angles, chances shall strike part her gunwale long." "Shall I go call men?" asked Billy. "They cooking breakfast, sir," observed Bird. "Let go means," said Tom; "if find boat come back afterwards dig her up." They immediately set work, Tom's directions, sand risen even higher supposed, boat's stretchers hands work with, slow business. "I have thought, sir, quicker way finding her this," observed Jerry; taking his axe, he cut short pole sharp point, ran though sand, along line Tom marked out. "There is something here, sir," he cried length, forthwith hole dug spot. Jerry plunged his hand. "No doubt it, sir; there is boat's side, weight sand bulged her out, she rights." "I fear score," observed Tom. "The sand probably driven around her, afforded her sides support. I thankful took precaution banking her did, I pretty sure she would rolled over, knocked pieces." The party satisfied safety boat, returned camp, found Tim Pat busily engaged huge fire cooking pork chops. "Why, come from?" asked Tom. "Shure, sir, porker found bush. It is belief it is baste Mr Desmond shot last night. He quite dead, showed fight, finished him, cut jiffy." "I congratulate success," said Tom. "To tell truth," said Desmond, "I half dreaming time; I quite sure morning whether I shot anything not, I am mighty glad find dream come true." The pork chops found satisfactory, still know abundance animal food island; one hog, would certainty many more; time, would prevented increase roots would otherwise afforded nourishment. "As hogs live here, there, probably acorns nuts various sorts, even cocoa-nuts bananas run short, need apprehension wanting vegetable diet," said Tom Desmond. "Again I say good reason thankful landed island abounding provisions." "I wish brought tea, coffee, sugar," said Billy. "I enjoyed breakfast much more." "Be thankful got," observed Tom. Before setting commence digging boat, Tom suggested form rough spades, without operation would tedious one. Having ascertained exact position boat, running pointed stick, commenced operations. They much surprised enormous pit dig even reached gunwale boat. The digging easy enough; labour consisted heaving sand sufficient distance. All hands getting hungry. Billy, usual, first cry out. "What say dinner, Rogers?" I would turned pork pretty quickly, I could get hold musket, scampered away back woods; we will even long. It appeared next instant creature's tusks would run him, he seized branch free threw upon it, animal ripped hem his broad trousers. Luckily canvas gave way, Pat would brought ground. The boar looked his late opponent he still meditated vengeance; suddenly seeing party cliff, he came towards them, tearing ground his fury, his sharp tusks. Fortunately musket loaded. This moment distracted his attention, and, instead coming directly Tom his companions, swerved little one side. Jerry sprang one side avoid charge, drove his boat-hook neck, bearing ground. On Tim Desmond sprang forward, and, could rise, dealt several heavy strokes axes, preventing committing mischief. "Hurrah; you have finished baste, I hope," cried Pat, watching proceedings his bough, came hurrying forward. "I would somehow missed couple pigs, I caught sight big fellow taking snooze sun. I creeping him, he opened his wicked eyes, I had not taken heels he would his tusks me. At last I stopped behind free gave shot; he did not mind all, all, reason bullet flew his head, I run it. However, `All's well ends well,' and, sure, supper, greatest pleasure world." After specimen rat's sportsmanlike qualities, Tom resolved trust musket again, necessary carefully husband powder shot. She moved, however, feet cut hollow she imbedded, object gained night putting her water, although bay smooth she might floated perfect safety. Tom made his usual visit Flag-staff Hill, came back report previous evening. "Before launch boat," he said, he rejoined party breakfast, "we must dismantle tent; indeed wise wear sail using roof. We may want it, shall certainly require oars. I therefore propose, ship appear noon, build hut place tent, shall shelter, require it, night. We cannot tell may need. The hurricane season yet over, may depend upon that. We came first blow, may several others weather becomes settled." "What! Do think ship's coming back us?" asked Billy, anxious tone. "I like change clothes, I wish tea sugar, hard tack, pepper, mustard, sorts things." "As ship's coming back, it is possible she may not," observed Tom. As soon breakfast over, oars gear boat carried beach, when, help rollers, she was, hands hauling together, labour, run water. As Tom feared might case, soon discovered that, either hot atmosphere pressure she subjected, she leaked considerably. The leaks, however, hoped, would partially fill up, though she would require fresh caulking, coat tar, substitute, tar procured. The hour noon approached, and, spite heat, Tom Desmond climbed flag-staff. They looked around horizon, other. "I afraid she come all," exclaimed Desmond. "I feared much first," answered Tom. "Then propose doing?" asked Desmond. "I do not wish live month month, tell year year, fellows fighting Chinese, rest world, perhaps." "No, I," said Tom. "We must fit boat well sea, try make way, either back Japan, Ladrones, bound; but, I said before, will not put sea hurricane season over. Even fine weather pretty long trip open boat; people gone far, much farther, others done do." "I ready anything think best," answered Desmond, "and I sure rest be, must try fit boat long voyage, sooner set better." "It difficult job without tools," observed Tom. "Faith, I forgot that," remarked Desmond. "Still, often say, `Where there is there is way.' As shall want sail, must try manufacture thick matting instead canvas, fix bows raise gunwale foot two, keep sea. Then provisions, shall salt many hogs kill, dry stock yams, carry water cocoa-nut shells." "I glad, Gerald, thought matter; that is I going propose," said Tom. "Of course," cried Gerald. "I thinking number things besides I digging sand, though I like talk time came action." Thus two midshipmen discussed plans future. On return camp, time fixed upon Tom passed ship arrived, tent dismantled Tom set men work cut poles sufficient length serve rafters uprights. Their tent answered well agreed hut roof shape. The walls formed closely interlacing uprights creepers, also served bind large pandanus leaves used covering roof. The hut nearly completed, Tom Desmond set out, armed muskets, try kill hog small game. Billy wanted go, Tom advised remain assist finishing hut. "If one fellows run you, could without weapon sort?" "But I would take boat-hook," said Billy. "A wild bear would afther laughing hands," observed Desmond. Though saw several hogs, animals seemed abound island, unable get near enough obtain fair shot. While search hogs, object also explore island. They made way across northern side. It consisted deep indentations high rocks, top one climbed; could make far distance another island north them. Though narrowly scanned ocean every direction, sail seen. "I determined give her altogether," said Tom; "but still, she escaped shipwreck, I cannot account commander coming look us. My idea mistake he supposes lost, driven long way southward, he think worth come far his course." On way back caught sight large number good-sized birds perched thickly tree, apparently intending roost night. Having drawn bullets, loaded small shot, firing midst birds, brought dozen, proved species pigeon. "We got something supper, events," cried Desmond he ran pick birds finish still fluttering ground. Their ill-success hog-hunting made determine next day go fishing boat. It need said either Tom Desmond paid periodical visits flag-staff. So often disappointed last gave expectation seeing ship. Their fishing excursion, though successful first, produced good supply fish, ate fresh rest dried sun smoked wood fire. They had, however, keep baling nearly whole time. This satisfied must caulk boat could venture sea her. All hands busily employed variety ways. Pat woven baskets long grass, Billy Tim, carrying one, went search salt, found plentiful supply hollows rocks, close sea. Tom Desmond searched directions trees might yield pitch gum description would serve pay outside boat, searched vain. "We must find substitute pitch, cannot accomplish voyage, that is certain," said Tom. The boat constantly kept wet; last tried sinking her several hours together, her planks would swell sufficiently stop leaks. They almost despair. "Had good supply powder, might live luxury fish, flesh, fowl, plenty vegetables; without powder, get continuance weather, may reduced vegetable diet," said Desmond, sitting round fire supper. "As hogs, may pretty sure catching them," observed Pat; "we soon find runs, digging pitfalls will not long porker find his way in." "Then sooner manage dig pitfall catch porker better," said Tom. "That thing I will set to-morrow morning, Tim mate," answered Pat. Tim agreed, arranged. "I like get half dozen hogs well salted smoked, may fear meat turning bad," said Tom; "we cannot tell long voyage may last, us run short provisions help it. We must also catch cure supply fish, they, yams, serve us provisions. Nothing else likely keep, though perhaps may obtain birds vegetables islands may pass." "But will not land, sir, unless know people inhabit them," said Pat. "Where I living long would knocked visitors head eaten up, certainty." "My belief people side equator generally well disposed towards strangers," said Tom. "I heard commander say short time ago, he reading books subject." So altogether Tom persuaded imbued his companions idea proposed voyage could performed without extraordinary risk, hands looked forward time might venture commence it--not tired remaining island--but even men wish spend days there, midshipmen naturally anxious employed active service. Next morning, Tom, gone usual flag-staff take look out, he descending, saw several dark objects moving sand bay him. Some far dry sand, others nearer water. Each man got hold stick weapon sort. The instinct turtle telling enemies approaching, farthest beach began make way, vigorously working fins, towards water. Tom Desmond, ahead, managed get sticks good-sized one, turned without much difficulty, attacked three others succession, throwing backs. The rest party come up. Jerry Tim, way, turned two more. Bidding farewell companions, first directed course towards south-east end island, which, rocky barren appearance, yet visited. CHAPTER THREE. TOM AND DESMOND DISCOVER A WRECK--HORRIBLE SCENE--FIND TOOLS AND STORES ON BOARD--RETURN WITH THEIR TREASURES TO THE CAMP--VISIT THE WRECK IN THEIR BOAT, AND BRING BACK STORES--THE BOAT FITTED FOR SEA--LAST NIGHT ON SHORE--SETTING SAIL--STEER FOR JAPAN--WIND CHANGES--STAND TO THE SOUTH--A LONG CALM--FOLLOWED BY A SHARK--A BREEZE, BUT AGAINST THEM-- RUNNING SHORT OF PROVISIONS--REDUCED TO YAMS AND OIL--BOAT RUN DOWN BY A WHALER--DESMOND AND TIM MISSING--TOM AND JERRY FIND THEM. Tom Gerald trudged manfully forward survey island. The path uneven. They kept near coast could, frequently could make way, account ruggedness rocks, turning inland. They clamber fallen trunks cut path axe thick creepers. At times climb wild rocks rugged hills, descend again, either valley running shore shore itself. Their object being, however, examine productions island, generally kept away beach. They made good eight ten miles, when, ascending rocky height, obtained view sea line coast distance. Suddenly Tom stopped put his hand his companion's arm. "Tell me, Desmond, think dark object there? It curiously shaped, like--or, it--" "A vessel, sure," exclaimed Desmond, whose eyes turned towards spot. "How could she come without seeing her?" "She may possibly time," said Tom. "Certainly she must wrecked gale landed here, she appears thrown high rocks." As got vessel, saw she driven shore two ledges, she remained fixed. It probably high tide she wrecked, water completely left her. After much difficulty, scrambling along rocks, midshipmen got alongside, hauled board ropes hanging bows. The vessel fore-top-sail schooner. Her masts still standing, her canvas hoisted, though torn tatters, fluttering breeze. A horrible odour came main hold went aft, looking horror see three bodies, one apparently white seaman, his dress, two evidently blacks, rags still hanging remains. The two midshipmen anxious accomplish survey vessel, hastened aft. About companion hatch bulwarks, wood chipped off, bullets, signs severe struggle taken place time board. They descended companion ladder; foot stains blood, traces discovered steps. They expected, odour pervaded whole vessel, find festering body cabin, human being, either dead alive, there. They discovered, however, evidently captain's log-book, shown vessel _Ark_, Brisbane, Queensland, she engaged carrying labourers various islands serve apprentices three years colony. How she come thus far north impossible say. The last entry log showed she latitude Caroline group; she deserted there, she must drifted several hundred miles. Tom Desmond concluded blacks must risen white crew, latter, defending desperately, must overcome, former probably swum shore. One thing certain, terrible tragedy enacted board. The dead bodies could tell tales; probably fallen struggle left companions. Perhaps blacks, murdering crew, steered northward, fancying islands lay direction. "We may suppose anything like," said Tom; "but shall get nearer truth. However, take care log, see anything got it. We see vessel contains anything likely useful, is, must send fetch without delay, another gale might knock her pieces." Before could continue search come take fresh air; descended little cabin. No sooner commenced search found set carpenter's tools, parcels nails, several articles required repairing boat. "These indeed treasures," said Tom, he examined them. "Now, find cask tar, shall fortunate." "That likely forward, hold," said Desmond. "Ugh! I do not like go hold," said Tom; "but must go down, find want forward." Nearly articles wanted cabin: quadrant, chart, canvas rope, sail-maker's needles, twine--indeed, almost everything could possibly require. They placed, ready packing up, things value them, tools, quadrant, chart, spy-glass, articles. They then, unwilling remain longer board necessary, made way forward. Almost one first objects eyes encountered examined fore hold cask tar, got apparently use; also oil, turpentine, white lead, brushes. "I wish time skill, might, instead repairing boat, built another better fitted intended voyage. Perhaps could get vessel off?" suggested Desmond. "You would say saw her high tide, water must flow her, her bottom like sieve," answered Tom. "We must think launching her, building another boat; may improve craft, make her thoroughly seaworthy." As tackles hand, hoisted tar-barrel deck; time impossible remain longer board, therefore, valuable articles two parcels, Tom first descended, Desmond lowered side him. Altogether packages weighed good deal; but, delighted acquisition, trudged along right merrily, hoping get back night. "We shall astonish them," exclaimed Desmond, "when see us things brought." They little difficulty getting back, frequently stop rest; eager join comrades, persevered, length, night closed them, caught sight welcome fire cliff. Day day shark followed boat, his hideous snout seen, triangular fin his, would useless put fishing-line, would certainly carried off. When, however, fresh provisions ran short, Gerald Tom determined try get rid fearful foe. The three men Billy, who, though fat short, pulled good oar, rowing men task many hours, sort mechanical fashion, Tom exclaimed-- "Load muskets, Desmond, cannot kill brute astern, get slices his carcase, will, events, drive away." The muskets kept clean ready use. They soon loaded, midshipmen, bringing weapons shoulders, took, thought, steady aim fired. The shark instantly sank sight. Whether hit not, could tell, possible bullets, deflected water, glanced clear his head. They reloaded, expecting he would return; though looked clear water astern either side, monster nowhere seen. "He will not trouble us again," said Desmond. "I feel pretty sure bullet went him." "And I think mine did," said Tom; "but neither could killed him, he would floated up." "Then sooner get lines try catch fish supper better," exclaimed Billy. Taking heavy leads, two lines baited pieces rancid pork allowed tow astern. The lines time, bite obtained. "Perhaps lines deep enough, bait good be," observed Desmond, beginning haul upon his line. He got third length, he felt torn his grasp, he caught sight monster running it. The next instant, Desmond line round thwart, snapped short off. Away went hook line. Directly after, Tom's line, hanging quarter, without warning snapped off. "It is brute shark come back again," cried Tom. "Get muskets, Desmond, entice near, settle time." "He is knowing that, sir," observed Jerry. "You may fire away every shot you have got--he would see coming, way reach him." Tom, believing this, determined try more. He got another piece pork, fastened end one broken lines. "The hooks puzzle his inside," said Desmond, "when he begins feel them. He will think twice he another bite." The muskets loaded, midshipmen standing up, kept eyes closely watching bait, floated surface, two three fathoms astern. "There he comes," cried Desmond. And shark, turning his back, exposed white his belly, fired. The brute disappeared, bait, sinking like rocket lost sight. "We finished time, events," cried Desmond. "He will take hooks." "Yes, lost slices his back," cried Billy; "and, unless catch fish, shall short commons supper." Hoping troubled shark, fresh lines got out. No fish, however, took bait; either none came near, suited tastes. Supper consequently consisted biscuits tea; warm tea great comfort heat day. The watch kept lines night, still without success. Two days went little variation. Now hopes raised seeing ripple far away surface; but, caused wind, died away reached them. They short allowance water; skins either evaporated leaked out, store cocoa-nuts soon exhausted, boat's breaker, already commenced. KINDLY TREATED ON BOARD THE AMERICAN WHALER--LOOKING OUT FOR WHALES--A WHALE KILLED--CUTTING IN AND TRYING OUT--THE MASTER GOES OFF IN CHASE-- THE SECOND MATE LOST OVERBOARD--SANDWICH ISLANDER ENDEAVOURS TO SAVE HIM--THE BOATS DISAPPEAR--NO APPEARANCE OF THE MASTER AND FIRST MATE--A GALE--THE BOATSWAIN ASSUMES COMMAND AND PLAYS THE TYRANT--WILL NOT SEARCH FOR THE CAPTAIN--HIDES THE NAUTICAL INSTRUMENTS--THE BOATSWAIN DASHES TOM'S QUADRANT TO THE DECK--NIGHT--THE MIDSHIPMEN TURN IN--THE SHIP STRIKES--BOATSWAIN AND CREW PUT OFF--LEAVE TOM AND HIS COMPANIONS ON THE WRECK--WEATHER MODERATES--LAND SEEN--THEY BUILD A RAFT--VOYAGE TO THE SHORE--SEE A SAVAGE ON IT--TURNS OUT TO BE PAT CASEY--NIGHT ON SHORE. As island uninhabited, Tom consider necessary set watch; indeed, one party made attempt, probabilities he would unable keep his eyes open. CHAPTER FIVE. SEARCH FOR AND FIND THE BOAT--RETURN IN HER TO THE WRECK--FIND MORE STORES, AND BUILD A RAFT--CARRY IT TO THE SHORE, AND GO BACK TO BREAK UP THE WRECK FOR BUILDING A VESSEL--ONCE MORE GETTING BACK THEY FIND THE DOCTOR WORKING AT A STILL--ANOTHER TRIP--IT COMES ON TO BLOW HARD--REACH SHORE--THE STILL SUCCESSFUL--THE GALE INCREASES--ITS EFFECTS ON THE WRECK--MORE STORES SAVED--SEEDS FOUND AND SOWN--A FLAG-STAFF SET UP-- PLANS FOR THEIR PROPOSED VESSEL--ENGAGED IN SHOOTING AND FISHING-- DISCOVER A MARINE POULTRY-YARD--BILLY AND THE EGGS--SUCCESSFUL FISHING-- SEEDS SOWN. Tom, always first foot, roused his companions. "Do let fellow his sleep out," murmured Billy; "we got nothing do." "We have plenty do," answered Tom. "We have got look water, find build hut, ascertain food island produces, try go back wreck bring stores, put flag-staff, fifty things." "Well, I did not think that," said Billy, sitting up. "Dear me, dear me! are, another desert island; chances remaining born days." "Better bottom sea, crunched sharks," observed Desmond, "or cast shore among cannibals, would cooked eaten us first opportunity. It barren island either, cocoa-nut trees, may fruits roots. We shall probably also able catch plenty fish." "If could get hold fine fat turtle, would purpose," said Billy. "Pat makes capital turtle soup. I am glad he escaped." "I afraid turtle done laying eggs time," observed doctor. "They come shore purpose, likely catch otherwise, must give thoughts revelling turtle." While Peter prepared breakfast, Pat climbed one cocoa-nut trees, sent nuts enough afford party refreshing draught liquid. It could properly called milk, yet assumed white appearance, nut perfectly ripe. It welcome, notwithstanding. Though small cask water brought shore, Tom wisely wished husband spring discovered. About doctor doubtful, Pat, he questioned subject, stated he discovered signs water. The sandy beach divided many places masses coral extending distance water, among boat might easily concealed. Had she, however, thrown them, she would, Tom feared, probability knocked pieces. The surprising thing Pat seen her. It appeared his account he partially recovered his senses, finding shore, he set confused state mind, without knowing he going, time must elapsed he came entirely himself. "Of course; may months years, may get days weeks. Had good carpenter among us, might built vessel wreck, she hold together long enough us bring good portion her planking timber ashore; I certain none us capable that, although stock carpenter's tools." What think it, Bird?" "Well, sir, I helped rig many craft, cannot say I ever worked shipwright, though I ready try hand anything else, `where there is there is way.'" "What say, Pat?" asked Tom. "As that, Mr Rogers, man Prime Minister, he ought think fit anything; sooner live dissolute island life, I would undertake build ninety-gun ship, I materials." The answers two seamen made Tom think Desmond's proposal was, events, worth consideration. "Well, find get timber enough wreck, I do not see make attempt," he said, turning matter his mind. "I will undertake build vessel ten fifteen tons, carry us Sandwich Islands," observed Desmond, confidently. "I got idea head, though I cannot promise she much clipper, she shall keep afloat, beat windward, stand pretty heavy sea." Tom Desmond discussed matter walked along. Presently Pat, started ahead, cried out, "Arrah! she is, right, tight," he pointed little sandy bay, almost extreme northern end island. There lay boat beach. She narrowly missed swept round island, she would probability lost unless counter current, lee side, driven her back. She escaped also another danger, dashed pieces rugged ledge close she must passed. The party hurried her ascertain damage she received. The surf evidently turned her over, little water remained her. At first sight she appeared uninjured. "I afraid so," said Tom, he going round her, put his hand hole bows. "The water ran here; perhaps she would suffered she thus damaged. "We shall bring tools materials here. And let us see oars cast shore." They hunted about, oars, much lighter boat, either swept round north end island thrown part shore. Having hauled boat up, returned towards camp. Tom Desmond anxious repair boat visit wreck night-fall, case weather change she go pieces. As walked along discussed best plan repairing boat. PROGRESS MADE IN BUILDING A VESSEL--TOOLS BREAK--SIGNAL KEPT FLYING--A SAIL SEEN--THE FLYING BEACON--A NIGHT OF SUSPENSE--SIGNAL GUNS FIRED--AN ANSWERING GUN HEARD--A MAN-OF-WAR STEAMER IN SIGHT--A BOAT COMES ON SHORE--TOM AND HIS FRIENDS GET ON BOARD HMS BELLONA, CAPTAIN MURRAY, AND FIND CAPTAIN ROGERS--FALL IN WITH A DISMASTED JUNK--JONATHAN JULL AND HIS WIFE--SUSPICIOUS APPEARANCE OF JUNK--JULL AND HIS WIFE TAKEN ON BOARD THE BELLONA--THE JUNK BLOWS UP AND FOUNDERS--THE BELLONA PROCEEDS ON HER COURSE--PASS A REEF--A WRECK SEEN--VISITED--SUPPOSED TO BE THE DRAGON--NO ONE FOUND ON SHORE--BELLONA REACHES HONG-KONG--JULL DISAPPEARS--CAPTAIN ROGERS ASSUMES COMMAND OF THE EMPRESS. The midshipmen doctor somewhat sanguine regard rapidity proposed craft could built. They taken account damage tools would receive unskilful hands. She length succeeded made her way boom. The moment she struck it, Chinese batteries opened her heavy guns. The gun-boats took stations astern her. A VISIT TO THE TAILOR'S, AND A WALK ROUND VICTORIA--TRICKS OF THE COOLIES--A CHINESE FESTIVAL--SAIL FOR SHANGHAI--AN UNEXPECTED MEETING-- ADVENTURES OF THE DRAGON'S CREW--A WALK THROUGH SHANGHAI--THE MIDSHIPMEN'S RIDE INTO THE COUNTRY--THEIR PLEASURE DISAGREEABLY INTERRUPTED--A RIDE FOR LIFE, AND A NARROW ESCAPE--BRING NEWS OF THE APPROACH OF THE REBELS--REGAIN THEIR HOTEL--AROUSED BY THE SOUND OF FIRING--SHANGHAI ATTACKED BY THE REBELS--THE BLUE JACKETS TAKE PART IN THE DEFENCE--TREACHERY DEFEATED--JERRY SAVES TOM'S LIFE--THE REBELS DEFEATED--RETURN ON BOARD THE EMPRESS--THE ORION, CAPTAIN ADAIR, ARRIVES FROM ENGLAND--ADAIR COMES ON BOARD THE EMPRESS--GERALD'S ANXIETY--AN ASTOUNDING REQUEST--CAPTAIN ADAIR COMMUNICATES SOME INTERESTING INFORMATION TO DESMOND--THE FLEET ASSEMBLES, AND THE ARMY LANDS ON THE SHORES OF CHINA. CHAPTER EIGHT. BELLONA AND EMPRESS IN VICTORIA HARBOUR--A COMPLAINT OF PIRACY--MR. JULL AGAIN--THE TWO SHIPS SAIL IN SEARCH OF HIS FLEET OF JUNKS--CAPTAIN PO-HO GOES AS PILOT--FAIL IN WITH ORION--ORDERED TO JAPAN--EXPEDITION TO ATTACK A PIRATICAL FLEET COMMANDED BY JULL--THE PIRATE FLEET SIGHTED-- TOM AND DESMOND SENT IN CHASE OF JUNKS--TOM HOARDS A JUNK, AND HAS GOOD REASON FOR GETTING OUT OF HER AGAIN--TOM, PURSUING THE ENEMY, IS CAPTURED--BILLY PULLS AFTER THE OTHER BOATS--THE FIRST JUNK BLOWS UP-- VAIN SEARCH FOR TOM--RETURN TO THE GNAT--THE FORT AND JUNKS ATTACKED-- THE ROUND MOON RECOVERED--JERRY RECOGNISES JULL--THE SEAMEN AND MARINES ON SHORE PREPARE TO ATTACK THE FORT. The Taku Forts captured, march Pekin accomplished, summer palace destroyed, pride emperor humbled, peace established. Her Majesty's ships _Bellona_ _Empress_ lay Victoria Harbour, broad pennant Commodore Murray, he lately raised rank, flying board former. He Captain Rogers seated cabin his ship dinner. The officers commodore's guests retired, midshipmen previously received polite hint go deck ascertain way wind blew. "I heartily hope shall soon ordered away undelectable coast," observed Jack. "So I, truth," answered Murray. "From I hear, shall soon sent Japan, seems unsettled state Mikado, Tycoon, Damios loggerheads. If latter especially put down, get upper hand two spiritual temporal sovereigns, set work murder other, whole country thrown state anarchy." "I glad something do, events," said Jack. "The gun-boats work nowadays, reduced Celestials order much prospect big ships wanted." "Had I reason proceeding definite direction I would sail to-morrow," observed commodore; "but object cruising coast, expending coals wearing ship." "I sometimes tempted wish steam power never introduced board men-of-war I think early days _Racer_ Mediterranean, life led coast Africa here," said Jack. "After all, youngsters best it." "They certainly cares responsibilities, enjoy sounder sleep command sea," observed Murray. While speaking, Archie Gordon, cap hand, entered cabin, addressing commodore said, "A Chinaman come board, sir, far understand, desires see report his junk time ago attacked carried pirates." "I see once; let come below," answered commodore. "Request Mr Chin-ho, interpreter, come here." "He gone shore, sir," replied midshipman. In less minute Gordon returned, ushering stout-built Chinaman, dressed, English eyes, unnautical costume, characteristic strange people. "What got say, friend?" asked Murray, visitor made usual salutation requested sit down, Murray properly made rule treat Chinese due courtesy. The stranger introduced Po-ho, captain big junk _Round Moon_. As curious jargon he made his statement would understood readers, must give ordinary English. "The _Round Moon_ lying Swatow roads, company several trading junks, I, asleep cabin, awakened loud noise deck, shrieks cries, clashing swords, scuffling thumps, though men falling. Rushing see matter, horror discover deck possession strangers, crew lay dead dying. My mate two three others still fighting bravely, far cabin door, I beheld Englishman, Jull name, I knew fearful scoundrel, sword covered blood his hand, attack mate others. Before I could run back get arms, Jull killed mate, rest cut down. Seeing I share fate, I jumped cabin port water, intending swim junk astern, Jull, followed cabin, discovering I overboard, fired me, missed. I thought I escape, presently another shot struck back; still I swam on, reached side junk. "When I got board, first thing I saw ship sails set, standing harbour. I wanted captain junk picked give chase, he answered, `No, no; Jull got many men long guns.' Before I could say anything I fainted. When I came myself, _Round Moon_ sight. I seen her since, wishing recover her, I ceased inquiring Jull every place I touched. A days ago, I sailing Chusan, I heard Jull, command large fleet junks, attacked plundered number merchant vessels neighbourhood, he even anchor his fleet channel island Latea Chusan. If go northward steamers, may arrive time catch he sails away. He nearly thirty junks, carrying heavy guns gingalls, 500 600 men. Your steamers cannot get creek attack him, he likely make his escape he knows coming. You must, therefore, send large force, careful approach, he fights rope round his neck, he struggle last." This narrative took long time deliver, Mr Po-ho, though he professed speak English fluently, search words express himself, Murray Rogers cross-question make repeat he said could comprehend his meaning. The above, however, said, substance his statement, reduced plain English. Murray inquired whether Mr Po-ho, rather Captain Po-ho, ready go pilot. He jumped offer. Nothing would give satisfaction see Jull's head cut off. "We go," said Murray. "Return board, Jack; hoist blue Peter, fire guns bring officers men may shore. I same, sail evening. Are ready, Captain Po-ho?" The Chinaman's little eyes twinkled satisfaction. "He would," he said, "send his boat back let his friends know he found generous Englishmen avenge his loss, expressed hope his junk recovered, she would restored him."
