THE MASTER OF THE FOX--BARGAIN FOR A PASSAGE--TRADING WITH THE NATIVES-- FAREWELL TO FRIENDS--THE SKIPPER'S RASCALLY TRICK--THE FOX WITH THE MIDSHIPMEN ON BOARD AT SEA--BAD FARE--FISHING--A SHARK CAPTURED, AND THE SKIPPER KNOCKED OVER--SHORT OF WATER--THE FOX STRUCK BY A SQUALL-- CAPSIZED--THE MIDSHIPMEN HOLD ON TO THE SIDE OF THE BRIG--IN A DESPERATE CONDITION--A SAIL--TAKEN OFF BY A BOAT FROM THE EMPRESS--FOX FOUNDERS-- WELCOMED ON BOARD--SYDNEY REACHED--A PLEASANT VISIT ON SHORE--BOUND FOR NEW ZEALAND. While midshipmen standing shore harbour boat put brig, came towards them. She pulled four hands, two blacks two Malays. A stout white man, broad-brimmed straw hat, evidently skipper, sat stern sheets. On landing, latter, looking hard them, surveying travel-stained, tattered uniforms, inquired-- "Where world come from?" "From side New Guinea," answered Tom. He briefly narrated adventures. "We want get Sydney, expect find ship. Can take us there?" he added. "That depends circumstances," answered skipper. "Can pay passage?" "We work it, events, I doubt captain pay sum agree to," said Tom. Tom like either manner appearance skipper. Of course he express his opinion, either words looks. "Are bound Sydney?" inquired Tom; "for, so, may come terms." "As that, I mind putting there, provided pay expenses. I thinking going south, I quite made mind," answer. "The _Fox_ fine craft, another chance getting Sydney, English port many months come. Few British traders touch here." "I see several Chinese junks Malay proas. We may chance getting Banda, Dutch port, Singapore," said Tom, determined done, he could help it, master _Fox_. "You wish board _Fox_ sail one craft, I tell you," said skipper. "Come, better close me, I will undertake land Sydney. What say 30 pounds head, payment provisions liquors consume? It mighty deal better sweltering hot place, chance knocked head, brought fever." They soon returned master _Fox_ standing watching them. "May I ask name?" said Tom. "Yes; it is Stubbins; I have reason ashamed it." "Well, Captain Stubbins, pay twenty pounds a-head ourselves, fifteen men, besides pound day provisions." "You sharp young gentlemen, I have opinion," said skipper. "If do not like terms stay wish accepted them. I shall away fortnight more, I came yesterday, get rid cargo take fresh one board." WARFARE IN NEW ZEALAND--BLUE-JACKETS FROM EMPRESS AND ORION LAND--A DESPERATE ATTACK ON A PAH--THE PAH CAPTURED--A NIGHT MARCH--THE PARTY LOSE THEIR WAY--GAIN THE TOP OF A HILL--BIVOUAC--ATTACKED BY A LARGE PARTY OF MAORIS--A GALLANT DEFENCE--MANY KILLED--TOM WOUNDED--NEARLY OVERWHELMED--JACK HOLDS OUT BRAVELY--SUCCOURED IN TIME BY ADAIR AND DESMOND--ASSAULT ON THE PAH--DESERTED BY THE GARRISON--A NIGHT MARCH TO ATTACK A VILLAGE--DESPERATE DEFENCE OF THE INHABITANTS--THE OLD CHIEF'S GRANDDAUGHTER--TIM PROPOSES TO SPLICE HER OFFHAND--THE END OF THE CONTEST--HOMEWARD BOUND--BILLY STRUCK BY MOON-BLINDNESS--A THUNDERSTORM--BILLY RESTORED TO SIGHT--THE ORION LOST SIGHT OF--THE EMPRESS REACHES SPITHEAD. THE BELLONA AND EMPRESS SAIL FOR ADEN--PART COMPANY--BELLONA FALLS IN WITH A MERCHANTMAN IN DISTRESS--A GLEAM OF HOPE--TOUCHES AT THE CAPE AND ADEN, AND PROCEEDS UP THE RED SEA--THE BELLONA REACHES ANNESLEY BAY-- JACK AND TOM LAND AT ZULLA--VISIT THE BRITISH CAMP--EXTENSIVE OPERATIONS GOING FORWARD--MARCH COMMENCED--INTERVIEW BETWEEN SIR ROBERT NAPIER AND THE PRINCE OF TIGRE--THE BRITISH ARMY ADVANCES TO ATTACK MAGDALA-- ENCOUNTERS THEODORE'S FORCES--DEFEAT OF THE ABYSSINIANS--THEODORE SENDS LIEUTENANT PRIDEAUX TO SIR ROBERT--ANXIOUS NEGOTIATIONS--THE CAPTIVES RELEASED--MOST OF THEODORE'S TROOPS LAY DOWN THEIR ARMS--THE KING HOLDS OUT--MAGDALA STORMED--THEODORE SHOOTS HIMSELF--THE FORTRESS DESTROYED-- RETURN MARCH--THE BELLONA SAILS FOR ADEN. As _Bellona_ approached, her battered condition became clearly visible; her boats gone, her bulwarks stove in, she lay mere wreck water; people seen her deck, even telescopes directed them, countenances appeared worn haggard stood leaning bulwarks gazing approaching man-of-war. The _Bellona's_ way stopped, boat lowered, Tom soon alongside wreck. "What ship that?" he asked, he pulled up. "The _Argo_, Captain Robson, Hong-kong. In Heaven's Dame, I trust render us assistance," said man, hollow voice. "We short provisions, consumed last drop water yesterday. We dying thirst, scarcely strong enough keep pumps going." A remained foot, looked ready sink. Two boats immediately lowered, Alick's, first ready, cask water put, he several additional hands returned merchantman. The fresh hands jumped board hoisted cask water, sight thirsty crew rushed aft. Tom, stood contents drawn up, hand cup master. He took hurried below. "It is his wife," observed one men; "she is bad." Beyond point, known Saddle Islamgi, rock fortress stood rose 300 feet height, precipitous sides, narrow, steep, winding path leading it, two lines defence, narrow gateway. The two brigades advanced, storming party leading, and, covered fire, steep path climbed scaling-ladders fixed, crowbars burst open gates. They met hot fire garrison, man could seen. Before stormers wall, surrounded strong thick barricade stout stakes, narrow stone gateway. On reaching gateway engineers, finding powder-bags forthcoming, immediately set work crowbars burst in, when, disappointment discover pile large stones, twelve feet height, still greater breadth, directly front them. All time exposed fire garrison. In vain endeavoured surmount formidable barricade, length party 33rd Regiment, turning right, discovered lower part wall, scaling-ladder placed. Immediately mounting, reached top wall, and, leaping down, forming so, attacked garrison, who, seeing fortress entered, took flight towards second defence. The whole regiment quickly in, and, pressing fugitives, rushed second gateway, when, summit fortress gained, British flag quickly flying it. On Abyssinians, throwing arms, asked quarter, granted. But become unhappy king, chief misery suffering endured his unhappy subjects many years? Stretched ground leading second gateway palace his body found, pistol-bullet his head, weapon he shot still his side. They all, however, long, driven back Gallas, watching side, compelled return fortress, delivered up. Taking possession Magdala, Sir Robert, made hasty survey it, collected Abyssinians centre space, placed strong guard them. An anxious night commenced, moment numberless thatched buildings covered heights might set fire heavy loss life ensued. The two gates carefully watched, and, owing admirable arrangements, disturbance occurred. The inhabitants desired take departure, body Theodore delivered his unhappy queen, interred two days afterwards church Magdala. The queen her son came British camp, received honourable treatment, inhabitants escorted far necessary towards district friends. The fortress afterwards destroyed, buildings within set fire, guns captured also burst fragments. THE EMPRESS LOSES SIGHT OF THE BELLONA--A GALE--SAILS BLOWN AWAY--RUNS BEFORE THE WIND--A LEAK--THE PUMPS MANNED--CREW SET TO BALE--PAT'S DREAM--PETE DISCOVERS THE LEAK--A THRUMMED SAIL GOT UNDER THE BOTTOM-- ANOTHER LEAK--THE GALE INCREASES--STEER FOR VIRGINIA ISLAND--ALL HANDS SPELL AND SPELL--THE SHIP PASSES OVER A REEF--FALSE KEEL CARRIED AWAY-- THE WATER GAINS ON THEM--ADAIR ADDRESSES THE CREW--THE MIDSHIPMAN AND SHIP'S BOY WITH THEIR WATER JUGS--LAND IN SIGHT--REACHED AT NIGHT--A BEACON FIRE APPEARS ON SHORE--SHIP DRIFTS FROM HER ANCHOR--SURMISES AS TO ITS BEING FLY-AWAY ISLAND--THE SHIP REGAINS AN ANCHORAGE--TWO BOATS SENT ON SHORE--GREEN GRASPS THE HAND OF LORD SAINT MAUR--STORES AND PART OF THE CREW LANDED--THE SHIP AGAIN DRIVEN OFF THE SHORE. We must go back _Empress_, left somewhere Tropic Capricorn, heavy gale wind, approaching hurricane. The donkey engine kept going, water hitherto considerably increased, still evident serious leak existed somewhere, although yet ascertained. Still, spite could done, water rose higher higher. "Peter," said Pat Casey his old shipmate, when, toiling four hours, knocked get little rest, "it is opinion last cruise I shall take together. I have many mighty quare fix now, niver one like this. Sure, there is nothing I hate ship hole her bottom, an' that is we have got, an' pretty big one, I am thinkin'." "You gib up, Pat," answered Peter. "We fall 'nother ship, sight land, get 'shore, stop de leak. When de cap'n finds de ship make much water, he keep her 'float fixin' sail her." "You may say ye plaise, sail could thrummed an' passed her keel, she will many fathoms depths ocean. An' supposin' fall ship, sure, could get aboard her sea runnin'? Then, reaching land-- where is land reach? I niver heard speak land away south'ard, except icy pole, an' niver see wished ever much." "Dat may de case; I nebber could make de meanin' ob chart, wheneber I hab de Pacific, find many islands, tink dere mus' here'bout. Why down-hearted?" "Down-hearted it, sure? I am down-hearted, Pater; I will tell ye, I dreamed dream night gale came on, I lay hammock; ould mither--who is gone glory six years--came stood side, an' I saw her face clearly I see yours, an' says she, `Tim, son, I have come wake you;' says I, `Mither, what is for?' Says she, `I wake ye well, although I cannot give ye dacent burial.' Upon she sit howlin' I thought would heard along deck. Says I, `Mither, hold fast there, you will afther disturbin' whole watch below.' But she would not, an' still howled on, jist I mind th' women ould Ireland whin I boy. Again I sung out, `Mither, ye love me, hold peace. I do not want waked now,' I uttered words I heard boatswain pipe hands deck, sure wind was not shrieking, an' blocks rattling, an' masts groaning, showin' dacent hurricane blowin'. Me mither vanished immediately, an' I tumbled deck, asleep thin awake, thinkin' good soul saying me." Peter fell asleep Pat talking, brief time summoned take spell baling. All efforts discover leak hitherto vain. Peter went chief engineer. "Pardon, sir, tink find de leak. If black Peter get drowned, easily find better man take place." LORD SAINT MAUR NARRATES HIS ADVENTURES--CARRIED OFF BY THE DUTCHMAN-- ILL-TREATED--DRUNKEN SKIPPER AND MATES--RIP VAN WINKLE AND SNARLEYOW-- SHIP STRIKE, ON A REEF--CREW DESERT HER--SAINT MAUR, RIP, AND SNARLEY GET INTO THE LONG-BOAT--SHIP GOES DOWN--REMAIN UNDER THE LEE OF THE REEF ALL NIGHT--MAKE SAIL IN THE MORNING--NO WATER--VIRGINIA ISLAND REACHED-- BOAT CAPSIZED ON THE BAR--SAINT MAUR AND RIP SAVED BY SNARLEY--THEIR LIFE ON THE ISLAND--WATER FOUND--GOAT'S FLESH--THE EMPRESS SEEN APPROACHING THE ISLAND--PREPARATIONS FOR CROSSING THE BAR--AWFUL SUSPENSE--SHIP STEAMS ON--STRIKES WITH A CRASH ON THE BAR--MORE STORES LANDED--THE JOLLIES ALARMED BY A JET OF STEAM--SAILS SEEN IN THE DISTANCE. "By-the-by, I never told I came playing Robinson Crusoe his man Friday yonder barren rock," observed Saint Maur, he his uncle paced together deck _Empress_. "You remember night I hooked yacht stranger ran us down, and, I thought, sent bottom. I leave judge state fear anxiety I left. From way fellows talked I got board, I discovered Dutchmen. I rushed aft skipper entreated heave lower his boats try pick might floating, he either understand would not. When I ran helm, intending put down, he might better comprehend meaning, he his mates held back. I pitched one fellow knocked over, treat way, skipper his big fist hit blow head brought deck. "When I came senses broad daylight, I knew long time, yacht gone down, must lost lives. I believe Dutchman intended apologise treated unceremonious fashion, but, I could understand word he said, I sure. He behaved, however, afterwards, far better I expected way acquaintance commenced. I never good hand picking languages, time I could make even imperfectly understood one board. Strange say, man among spoke word English. I wanted skipper put port, he replied that, `Out his course he would go man.' I begged him, chiefly signs, fall homeward-bound ship, put board her. He nodded his head let understand that, providing calm weather, he objection, advised meanwhile console his schiedam, he plentiful supply. Both he his mates indulged pretty largely, I found. I expected he would touch Cape, disgust he ran south'ard, order fall westerly trades, I found he intended touch nowhere he reached Batavia. "This anything consolatory, besides I one talk to, book board I could read. I tried hard make Dutch books he board, used ask mates, indeed men I found hand, pronounce words, I tried discover meaning. I believe, voyage lasted longer, I learned speak read Dutch fluently; but, skipper drunk half his time, mates two quarters, I could get much them. The fellow really use young Rip Van Winkle. He took liking me, I him, first, I often saved many cuff kick he will not receive crew. He was, I confess, sort `dirty Dick' board, he would continued I taught clean himself; he fond washing one, except weather cold, he rather objects it, falls back his bad habits. My companion besides Rip large dog--no great beauty--whom I called Snarleyow, unable pronounce his Dutch name, he took it, he me, immediately, always came called. I treated friend, whereas, skipper downwards, he accustomed receive kicks ha'pence, except poor Rip, consequently great affection his masters. "Besides anxiety you, disappointment able take advantage new position which, Counsellor McMahon, I placed--not weighed much me--I could help feeling anxious way ship navigated. Being unable understand Dutch books, I could work reckonings, though frequently I took observation, keep hand in. "I chance communicating England. We sighted British ship, time I picked enough Dutch use signal-book, I hoisted signals `British officer board; heave him.' I thought skipper saw ship heave he would same, blowing hard, he obstinately refused lift tack sheet lower boat, fancy I felt I saw homeward-bound vessel standing away us. From temperature weather I suspected got long way south, came blow hard. The Dutchman shortened sail, he generally wind, continued course he steering. The old ship, though tub, good sea boat, I reason fear danger, provided she run her stem iceberg strike rocks reefs. Blow high, blow low, skipper walked deck his hands his pockets huge meerschaum his mouth, looking composed usual? "One night I turning in, I felt ship strike. Of course I sprang deck, I followed skipper first mate, second mate watch. The crew singing lost. "`Do afraid, boys!' cried skipper, calling light his pipe, thrusting his hands his pockets. `She will drive it. Another hand helm. Keep standing!' "I knew, thickness his voice, he half seas over, he never exhibited his state way, except he sank table. Still, I hoped his composure he knew were, scrape clear sand-bank sea breaking fearful force. Several seas, indeed, nearly pooped us; surged forward, touching occasionally way threatened split ship fragments; she held together wonderfully. The men, however, hope I had; I saw gathering either side, near boats, taking falls hands, ready lower without orders. "Rip came me. `What is going happen, mynheer?' he asked. "`The ship probably go bottom get knocked pieces; may perhaps escape danger, last reach Batavia,' I answered. `Whatever happens, stick me, Rip, lend hand whenever I want it, I may perhaps save you.' "Scarcely, however, I spoken ship struck far greater force before, fore main masts going board, falling clear deck. Still she went on; carpenter sounded well, found water rushing rate precluded possibility keeping ship afloat. She gone edge reef, rose starboard bow, high water, broke force sea. Springing aft, I put helm, man deserted, she rounded lee rocks. "The crew instantly began lowering boats. The skipper his first mate tumbled one, several men shoved off; second mate took possession other, rest crew, leaving Rip still deck. So overcrowded they, I saw likely go down; I determined take chance ship, I thought, light cargo board, might possibly float long enough enable us build raft. The two boats quickly disappeared darkness, without provisions water, men hurry forgot take, skipper his first mate drunk think it. I bethought examining boat amidships, I feared might crushed falling mast; fortunately escaped. I told Rip cut lashings clear, reminding lives depended it--to see rope remained attached vessel's deck. I jumped in, followed Rip Snarley, left board us, whose instinct showed boat likely prove ark safety. The oars, well masts sails, stowed her, couple hen-coops, last surviving pig, variety articles. The ship go immediately; I suspect that, hands remained board, might kept her afloat daylight, events. "We got oars shove boat clear instant water rushed deck. I think I ever experienced anxious moment life. At last sea came sweeping along, round reef, lifted us clear, right bulwarks, free masts spars still hanging side. We pulled away lives, saw masts dragged ship went bottom. The mizzenmast remained last water. We pulled lee reef; but, anchor, compelled hold her her position paddling night. When morning broke, land sight; wind westward, I judged safest plan steer northward, might either fall ship, make Java, western coast Australia, sight island way. We small cask water boat, three empty casks, put way. My hope able fill rain water got northern latitude, likely meet ship. The reef lay ran half mile north south water; much I could judge line white foam extended far eye could reach. As place ship likely approach, sooner got latitude better. The wind moderated, accordingly made sail stood eastward. "We three days boat, small cask water gradually diminishing, drop rain fallen fill casks, sighted small island. Hoping might afford us shelter, events might obtain water, steered towards it. As approached saw harbour opening us. Though I thought would risk crossing bar, yet I determined make attempt. Anything better dying thirst. The water appearing smoother centre, I stood sail boat could carry towards it, still blowing fresh. The bar reached; I expected next instant smooth water, abominable roller came tumbling in, swamped boat, turned her over, washing Rip away. I clambered bottom, I saw Snarley, come surface. The dog, looked him, made towards point inside harbour, and, exerting his strength, hauled Rip up. I, meantime, tossing bar, expecting every moment washed off, I saw Snarley returning. Knowing I his help, I sprang swam towards him. I twisted fingers left hand his long, shaggy hair, he towed surf safely shore, I found Rip already recovered waiting me. He threw his arms around neck burst tears, exclaiming Dutch--`I thought gone, mynheer, I left alone; come shall manage live.' "He bestowed his caresses Snarley saved me. The sun bright warm, soon dried clothes; exist next question, eaten pig, doomed quickly die satisfy hunger. I fancy raw pork, although companions particular. Suddenly I bethought wreck I put tin box matches pocket light pipe. I felt it. It there; although water got in, I hoped sun would restore efficiency. We looked about, trusting cask still remaining might sent us, nowhere seen. "`Patience,' I observed; `we may shower long, fill cask, bring safe.' The boat, I said, tumbling bar. At length driven inside harbour. Rip offered swim tow her in. I hesitated fear sharks, he declared latitude likely found. I begged wait she got nearer, she soon did, stripping his clothes, he boldly plunged in. "`You remain shore, mynheer,' he said; `you better able help come now. Should I get tired, I always rest bottom boat.' "When Snarley saw set off, he also plunged in. On reaching boat Rip put rope dog's mouth, taking another himself, began tow boat towards beach. It hard work, though wind partly favour, time sending boat towards foot cliffs opposite entrance, surf broke heavily, would soon knocked her pieces. By time, however, thirst became almost unbearable. "`Perhaps water may found hollows rocks,' observed Rip. "Snarley apparently suffering much were, he saw us moving away landing-place he ran ahead. "`He will find water, there is found,' said Rip; I hope. We climbed rocks, exertion reached top island, Snarley dashed forward, great joy saw his head hollow, evidently enjoying draught water. Trips also taken ship every day, long anything remained board get her. CHAPTER NINETEEN. CAPTAIN ADAIR'S LAST VISIT TO THE EMPRESS--RESOLVES TO BUILD A VESSEL OUT OF THE WRECK--THE DOCTOR FEARS THAT THE ISLAND MAY BE BLOWN UP--A HURRICANE--THE BOATS GET ADRIFT--THE SEA WASHES UP THE BEACH--A FLASH OF LIGHTNING REVEALS THE SHIP PARTING AMIDSHIPS--THE MASTS FALL--THE SHIP BREAKS UP--AN EARTHQUAKE--ROCKS FAIL FROM THE CLIFFS--RAFTS CONSTRUCTED--THE BOATS LAUNCHED--A STILL MORE FEARFUL CONVULSION THAN BEFORE OCCURS--THE CREW EMBARK ON THE RAFTS AND IN THE BOATS--ROY LEFT ON THE CLIFF--SAINT MAUR RETURNS TO CALL HIM--A FEARFUL RUSH FOR THEIR LIVES--REACH THE GIG IN TIME--THE ISLAND IN A TERRIFIC STATE OF COMMOTION--A SAIL IN SIGHT--APPROACHES THE ISLAND--PROVES TO BE THE BELLONA--ALL SAFE ON BOARD--TOUCHES AT THE CAPE--THE LAST OF MAJOR BUBSBY--ARRIVAL AT HOME--HAPPY MEETINGS--CONCLUSION. Adair Desmond paid visit _Empress_ one bright morning, harbour smooth mill pond, scarcely ripple even seen expanse ocean outside. She lay firm ever, her masts standing, appearance good condition she day attempt made bring her harbour, except looked could see clear water washing her. At distance she might supposed anchor. "I thinking vessel come near us since here, might wait months, perhaps years more, unless make attempt get means disposal," observed Adair. "What, would try cross Indian Ocean boats, would you?" asked Saint Maur. "No; I would thus risk lives people, must endeavour build craft wreck large enough get far Batavia, even Madras Calcutta," answered Adair. "I hopes first came shore ship would shortly appear, I decided building vessel. I determined delay longer. When return I draw plan carrying intention effect." Adair took several turns along deck. "This third ship I lost, I suppose I shall never get another," he said, sigh. "I shall looked upon unlucky man, though neither case could I blame myself, could one blame me. We go shore." He stepped accommodation ladder, still remained side. Some time spent consulting carpenter making arrangements pulling old ship pieces. Next morning hands begin work. It likely prove long undertaking, one sailor likes engaged in. It also doubtful weather would continue fine enough enable completed. During day slight movement earth felt, rumbling noise sounded beneath feet, another jet steam burst forth orifice distance town. But ship's company become accustomed sight spouts, trouble matter. In evening, Adair Desmond seated together, doctor called upon them. "I come, Captain Adair, state I made anxious days past various phenomena I observed island. I cannot help fearing internal commotion taking place beneath feet, may produce serious consequences. The orifices steam observed makes escape may prove safety valves, larger quantity steam engendered let off?" "You mean say, doctor, fear island may blown up, shall blown it?" said Adair, laughing, though he feel altogether comfortable his mind subject. "Such, captain, I apprehend may case, whether shortly time hence I cannot take upon say," observed doctor. "I would urge vessel built embark, I like leave human run risk destroyed, would case convulsion I dread take place." "That is thing fast possible," said Adair. The carpenter considers take us two months least break ship build new craft materials, hope land remain quiet task accomplished. They set once, still sufficient daylight enable reach spot doctor alluded. It came suddenly clap thunder, ere long breakers could heard roaring dashed rocky coast. Already wind lashed surface harbour foam, water rushed beach, threatening carry boats, largest moored short distance off, others hauled sand. The captain officers first aroused sound gale. They hurried out, turned hands secure boats. This easy matter, two already broken adrift, necessary risks go them. They, however, brought back full fury hurricane burst island. They length hauled beach means rollers placed strength fifty hands least applied each. The sea continued rise, became necessary drag still danger washed away. The largest boats still remained beach, men, headed captain, accompanied several officers, attempting drag her up, loud sound, like report heavy gun, heard. "There goes old ship!" cried several voices. Adair feared remark true. Scarcely words uttered, flash lightning revealed ship parting asunder amidships. The mizzenmast fell time, mainmast seen still standing. In another minute came mainmast crash, followed shortly afterwards foremast bowsprit, and, high roar surf howling wind, rending crashing ship's timbers could distinguished. The gale went increasing, sad sounds ship breaking continued, huge fragments cast force waves beach, several striking stern large boat, almost staving her she could hauled danger. Though men could more, stood watching catastrophe which, though many long expected it, come last suddenly upon them. As thus stood grouped together felt earth rock beneath feet way never done before. Then came sound far louder yet heard. Several men cried island blowing up. At moment fearful crash, light another flash lightning glimpse caught huge mass rock descending summit hill water. Another another followed. Adair Saint Maur remembered doctor's prognostications, began truly fear whole island breaking up, ere long might present mass broken fragments sink bodily beneath sea. They endeavoured, notwithstanding, maintain composure restore confidence men, many greatly alarmed. "Whatever becomes high cliffs seem crumbling away, I consider we, level spot, every chance escaping," exclaimed Adair. Though he obtain ship, he accompanied expedition Coomassie, took active part exploit redounded greatly honour troops, blue-jackets, marines engaged it, well noble leader, proving stern discipline courage effect, even pestiferous climates hosts brave foes.
